   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    List of S&amp;P 500 companies
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>
    <div id="jump-to-nav">
    </div>
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">
     Jump to navigation
    </a>
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">
     Jump to search
    </a>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Wikimedia list article
      </div>
      <p>
       The
       <b>
        S&amp;P 500
       </b>
       <a href="/wiki/Stock_market_index" title="Stock market index">
        stock market index
       </a>
       , maintained by
       <a href="/wiki/S%26P_Dow_Jones_Indices" title="S&amp;P Dow Jones Indices">
        S&amp;P Dow Jones Indices
       </a>
       , comprises
       <b>
        505
       </b>
       <a href="/wiki/Common_stock" title="Common stock">
        common stocks
       </a>
       issued by
       <b>
        500
       </b>
       <a href="/wiki/Market_capitalization" title="Market capitalization">
        large-cap
       </a>
       companies and traded on American stock exchanges (including the 30 companies that compose the
       <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">
        Dow Jones Industrial Average
       </a>
       ), and covers about 80 percent of the American equity market by capitalization. The index is weighted by free-float market capitalization, so more valuable companies account for relatively more of the index. The index constituents and the constituent weights are updated regularly using rules published by S&amp;P Dow Jones Indices. Although the index is called the S&amp;P 500, the index contains 505 stocks because it includes two share classes of stock from 5 of its component companies.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-2">
         [2]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

      <h2>
       <span id="Selected_changes_to_the_list_of_S.26P_500_components">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Selected_changes_to_the_list_of_S&amp;P_500_components">
        Selected changes to the list of S&amp;P 500 components
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_S%26P_500_companies&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Selected changes to the list of S&amp;P 500 components">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       S&amp;P Dow Jones Indices updates the components of the
       <a href="/wiki/S%26P_500_Index" title="S&amp;P 500 Index">
        S&amp;P 500
       </a>
       periodically, typically in response to acquisitions, or to keep the index up to date as various companies grow or shrink in value.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">
        <a href="#cite_note-6">
         [6]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Between January 1, 1963 and December 31, 2014, 1,186 index components were replaced by other components.
      </p>
      <table class="wikitable sortable" id="changes">

         <th rowspan="2">
          Reason
         </th>
